       for (var i = 1; i < tiles.length; ++i) {\n                if (tiles[i].getBoundingClientRect().top > rootTop)\n                  return i;\n              }\n              return 0;\n itemsPerRow; ++i) {\n                ys.push(0);\n              }\n              var rowCount = Math.floor((tiles.length + itemsPerRow - 1) / itemsPerRow);\n              for (var rowIndex = 0; rowIndex < rowCount; ++rowIndex) {\n                var maxY = Math.max.apply(null, ys);\n                for (var i = 0; i < itemsPerRow; ++i) {\n                  var tile = tiles[itemsPerRow * rowIndex + i];\n                  if (!tile) {\n                    // Incomplete row. All done!\n                    return;\n                  }\n                  tile.style.marginTop = '8px'; // no-op unless redoing because of window resize\n                  var rect = '' + marginTop + 'px';\n                  }\n                  ys[i] += rect.height;\n                }\n              }\n            }\n            layoutTiles();\n            var timeout = null;\n
